D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, Ubuntu One, your own Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): To use it, set Sync Service to Tomboy Web in preferences then  provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  455): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  455): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): See http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the notes' location on other platforms.
D/nofatclips(  455):

D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, Ubuntu One, your own Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): To use it, set Sync Service to Tomboy Web in preferences then  provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  455): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  455): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.

D/nofatclips(  456): Tomboy Web
D/nofatclips(  456): Tomboy Web is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, Ubuntu One, your own Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): To use it, set Sync Service to Tomboy Web in preferences then  provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  456): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  456): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  456): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): See http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the notes' location on other platforms.

D/nofatclips(  456): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  456): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  456): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): See http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the notes' location on other platforms.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): Back to Tomdroid
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): Quick mentions to tell you that unfortunately Tomdroid can't edit notes for now but this will come. Thanks for your patience.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): Also, Tomdroid is always looking for new contributors. If you are interested join the tomdroid-dev team on launchpad: http://launchpad.net/~tomdroid-dev.
D/nofatclips(  456): 
D/nofatclips(  456): Lastly, if you encounter any issue, please report it at: https://bugs.launchpad.net/tomdroid

D/nofatclips(  455): Welcome to Tomdroid!
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): You have no notes here yet. To get started, set your Synchronization preferences under Settings. There are two synchronization options described below.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Warning: Changing synchronization service will empty your note list.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, Ubuntu One, your own Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): To use it, set Sync Service to Tomboy Web in preferences then  provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  455): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  455): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): See http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the notes' location on other platforms.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Back to Tomdroid

D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Lastly, if you encounter any issue, please report it at: https://bugs.launchpad.net/tomdroid

D/nofatclips(  455): Welcome to Tomdroid!
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): You have no notes here yet. To get started, set your Synchronization preferences under Settings. There are two synchronization options described below.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Warning: Changing synchronization service will empty your note list.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, Ubuntu One, your own Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): To use it, set Sync Service to Tomboy Web in preferences then  provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  455): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  455): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): See http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the notes' location on other platforms.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Back to Tomdroid
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Quick mentions to tell you that unfortunately Tomdroid can't edit notes for now but this will come. Thanks for your patience.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Also, Tomdroid is always looking for new contributors. If you are interested join the tomdroid-dev team on launchpad: http://launchpad.net/~tomdroid-dev.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Lastly, if you encounter any issue, please report it at: https://bugs.launchpad.net/tomdroid

D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): To use it, set Sync Service to Tomboy Web in preferences then  provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  455): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  455):

D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  455): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.

D/nofatclips(  455):

D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Web is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, Ubuntu One, your own Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): To use it, set Sync Service to Tomboy Web in preferences then  provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  455): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  455): Ubuntu One - https://one.ubuntu.com/notes
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  455): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. The notes can be found in ~/.local/share/tomboy/ on Linux. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): See http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the notes' location on other platforms.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Back to Tomdroid
D/nofatclips(  455):

D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Also, Tomdroid is always looking for new contributors. If you are interested join the tomdroid-dev team on launchpad: http://launchpad.net/~tomdroid-dev.
D/nofatclips(  455): 
D/nofatclips(  455): Lastly, if you encounter any issue, please report it at: https://bugs.launchpad.net/tomdroid
